### Introduction Event

country_event = { # Intro Pt 1
	id = gerdom.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.1" }
	title = gerdom.1.t
	desc = gerdom.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Victory_March_Painting

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = gerdom.1.a
		country_event = gerdom.1001
	}
}

country_event = { # Hans von Seeckt dies
	id = gerdom.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.2" }
	title = gerdom.2.t
	desc = gerdom.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Seeckt_Grave

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = gerdom.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_army_reform
		set_country_flag = Hans_von_Seeckt_dead
		set_country_flag = August_Von_Mackensen_dead
		remove_ideas = GER_Hans_von_Seeckt_cos_pau
		remove_ideas = GER_August_Von_Mackensen_carm_pau
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_unit_leader = 983 }
					random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 983 }			
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_unit_leader = 9836 }
					random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 9836 }			
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Agricultural Crisis in the Völkerbund
	id = gerdom.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.11" }
	title = gerdom.11.t
	desc = gerdom.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Poor_Farmers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #refuse aid
		name = gerdom.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_political_power = 20
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER.GER_mitteleuropa_strength_var
			value = 3
			tooltip = sub_3_from_mitteleuropastrength_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_recalculate_mitteleuropa_effects = yes
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = GER_raised_tarrifs
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = WHR
			modifier = agriculture_help_denied
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = agriculture_help_denied
		}
		UKR = { country_event = ukreco.2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_angry_ukraine
	}

	option = { #promise aid
		name = gerdom.11.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_agricultural_mitteleuropa_help_tt
		set_country_flag = GER_helped_mitteleuropa_partners
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER.GER_mitteleuropa_strength_var
			value = 5
			tooltip = add_5_to_mitteleuropastrength_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_recalculate_mitteleuropa_effects = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = agriculture_help_granted
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = WHR
			modifier = agriculture_help_granted
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = agriculture_help_granted
		}
		UKR = { country_event = ukreco.3 }		
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GER_agricultural_aid_to_eastern_europe
			days = 105
		}
	}
}

### Suffrage movement

country_event = { # The increasing activity of the suffragist movement - triggered by CoF event
	id = gerdom.12
	title = gerdom.12.t
	desc = gerdom.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_suffrags
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.12" }
	
	trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_Springtime_in_Germany } }

	option = { # full
		name = gerdom.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ENG
			modifier = women_yes
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = women_yes
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = women_yes
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = women_yes
		}
	}

		name = gerdom.12.b

			factor = 70
		}
		add_political_power = -50

			target = ENG

		}

country_event = { # German women demand recognition for their war effort #REDO
	id = gerdom.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.13" }
	title = gerdom.13.t
	desc = gerdom.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_women

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		controls_state = 64
		controls_state = 51
		controls_state = 52
		NOT = {
			country_exists = FRA
			has_completed_focus = GER_Who_Leads_the_Cause_for_Women
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.13.a
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

	id = gerdom.15

		name = gerdom.15.a
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = tirpitz_battleship
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {

				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.15.b
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = tirpitz_carrier
			value = 1
		}

			}

			value = 1

# Time to review the program!

country_event = {
	id = gerdom.16
	title = gerdom.16.t
	desc = gerdom.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_ship

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owns_state = 58 #must own Kiel
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.16"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = tirpitz_battleship
						value > 1
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = tirpitz_built_battleships
					}
					controls_state = 58
				}
				load_oob = GER_BB_1
				load_oob = GER_BB_2
				set_country_flag = tirpitz_built_battleships
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = tirpitz_carrier
						value > 1
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = tirpitz_built_carriers
					}
					controls_state = 58
				}
				load_oob = GER_CA_1_naval
				load_oob = GER_CA_2_naval
				set_country_flag = tirpitz_built_carriers
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = tirpitz_destroyer
						value > 0
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers1
					}
					controls_state = 58
				}
				load_oob = GER_Z_1
				set_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = tirpitz_destroyer
						value > 1
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers2
					}
					controls_state = 58
				}
				load_oob = GER_Z_2
				set_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = tirpitz_destroyer
						value > 2
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers3
					}
					controls_state = 58
				}
				load_oob = GER_Z_3
				set_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = tirpitz_sub
						value > 0
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = tirpitz_built_subs1
					}
					controls_state = 58
				}
				load_oob = GER_U_1
				set_country_flag = tirpitz_built_subs1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = tirpitz_sub
						value > 1
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = tirpitz_built_subs2
					}
					controls_state = 58
				}
				load_oob = GER_U_2
				set_country_flag = tirpitz_built_subs2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.a
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = tirpitz_battleship
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = tirpitz_battleship
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.b
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = tirpitz_carrier
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = tirpitz_carrier
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.c
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = tirpitz_destroyer
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = tirpitz_destroyer
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.e
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = tirpitz_sub
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = tirpitz_sub
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.f
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_battleship
				value < 2
			}
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = tirpitz_battleship
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.g
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_carrier
				value < 2
			}
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = tirpitz_carrier
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.h
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_destroyer
				value < 3
			}
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = tirpitz_destroyer
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.i
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_sub
				value < 2
			}
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = tirpitz_sub
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.j
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 58
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_battleship
				value > 1
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_carrier
				value > 1
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_destroyer
				value > 2
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = tirpitz_sub
				value > 1
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_battleship
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_built_battleships
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_carrier
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_built_carriers
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_destroyer
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers1
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers2
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_built_destroyers3
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_sub
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_built_subs1
		clr_country_flag = tirpitz_built_subs2
		set_country_flag = navy_1934_complete
	}

	option = {
		name = gerdom.16.k
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 58
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.16
				days = 180
			}
		}
	}
}

### New Black Monday Stuff

country_event = { # Economic Flight
	id = gerdom.17
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.17" }
	title = gerdom.17.t
	desc = gerdom.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Ocean_Liners
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = gerdom.17.a
		add_stability = -0.04
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER.GER_mitteleuropa_strength_var
			value = 5
			tooltip = sub_5_from_mitteleuropastrength_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GER_has_black_monday
			GER_recalculate_mitteleuropa_effects = yes
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.19
				days = 12
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.14
				days = 25
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Reichstag Dissolved by Bundesrat

country_event = { #hidden event to trigger Wilhelm's death even if GER is dead
	id = gerdom.4700
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.4700" }
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = 64.owner #this needs to be a MTTH due to the variance in GER scenarios
		date > 1941.6.4
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = Wilhelm_II_Dead
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Wilhelm II" }
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = gerdom.47 }
			random_country = {
				news_event = { id = worldnews.235 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GEX = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			GEX = { country_event = gerdom.47 }
			GER = { GER_wilhelm_ii_dies = yes }
			random_country = {
				news_event = { id = worldnews.235 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			GER = { GER_wilhelm_ii_dies = yes }
			GEX = { GER_wilhelm_ii_dies = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CEA = {	
					has_country_flag = CEA_RESTORED_MAF
					GEX_fled_to_us = yes
				}
			}
			CEA = {
				country_event = {
					id = cea.27
					days = 55
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { LEP = { has_country_flag = AOG_willyii_gang } }
				LEP = { country_event = aogdeathevent.1 }
			}
			UKR = { country_event = ukrfor.154 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # resetting elections
	id = gerdom.210
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.210" }
	trigger = {
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = GER_1937_elections_cancelled
			has_country_flag = GER_1942_elections_cancelled
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

				var = GER_reichsexekution_success

				compare = equals
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23627
			days = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Middling
		name = gerdom.23626.b
		trigger = {

				var = GER_reichsexekution_success
				value = 2
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23628
			days = 1
		}
	}

		name = gerdom.23626.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_reichsexekution_success
				value = 1
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23629
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.23664" }
	title = gerdom.23664.t
	desc = gerdom.23664.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_GER_reichstag
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Ulrich von Hassell (Wrong)
		name = gerdom.23664.a
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23665
			days = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Erich Koch-Weser (Wrong)
		name = gerdom.23664.b
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23666
			days = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Heinrich Langwost and the German-Hanoverian Party (Right)
		name = gerdom.23664.c
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23667
			days = 2
		}
		add_to_variable = { GER.GER_reichsexekution_success = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Reichsexekution Prussia - Diplomacy Finale
	id = gerdom.23668
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.23668" }
	title = gerdom.23668.t
	desc = gerdom.23668.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_GER_reichstag
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Success
		name = gerdom.23668.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_reichsexekution_success
				value = 3
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23669
			days = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Middling
		name = gerdom.23668.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_reichsexekution_success
				value = 2
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23670
			days = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Failure
		name = gerdom.23668.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_reichsexekution_success
				value = 1
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.23671
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.304" }
	title = gerdom.304.t
	desc = gerdom.304.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Movie_Theatre
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Masterpiece
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_DkP_Movie_Success
				value = 3
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		name = gerdom.304.a
		country_event = gerdom.305
	}
	
	option = { # Good
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_DkP_Movie_Success
				value = 2
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		name = gerdom.304.b
		country_event = gerdom.306
	}
	
	option = { # Middling
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_DkP_Movie_Success
				value = 1
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		name = gerdom.304.c
		country_event = gerdom.307
	}
	
	option = { # Bad
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = GER_DkP_Movie_Success
				value = 0
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		name = gerdom.304.e
		country_event = gerdom.308
	}
}

country_event = { # Teutonic Middle
	id = gerdom.333
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.333" }
	title = gerdom.333.t
	desc = gerdom.333.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Ostsiedlung
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # German-Exclusive
		name = gerdom.333.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_Teutonic1A_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_Teutonic1A_idea
				add_idea = GER_Teutonic2A_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_Teutonic1B_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_Teutonic1B_idea
				add_idea = GER_Teutonic2B_idea
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.334
			days = 14
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Wide-Reaching
		name = gerdom.333.b
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_Teutonic1A_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_Teutonic1A_idea
				add_idea = GER_Teutonic2C_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_Teutonic1B_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_Teutonic1B_idea
				add_idea = GER_Teutonic2D_idea
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = gerdom.335
			days = 14
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # NLP Chain End
	id = gerdom.3525
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.3525" }
	title = gerdom.3525.t
	desc = gerdom.3525.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Ostsiedlung
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Await Results...
		name = gerdom.3525.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER_AfriCola_Success
					value = 4
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.3526
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER_AfriCola_Success
					value = 2
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.3527
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER_AfriCola_Success
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.3528
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER_AfriCola_Success
					value = 0
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.3529
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = gerdom.3593
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.3593" }
	title = gerdom.3593.t
	desc = gerdom.3593.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Ostsiedlung
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Heavy
		name = gerdom.3593.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER.GER_infiltration
					value = 2
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.3596
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER.GER_infiltration
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.3597
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER.GER_infiltration
					value = 0
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.3598
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				MAF = { exists = yes }
				GEA = { exists = yes }
				MAG = { exists = yes is_in_faction_with = GER }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MAF = { exists = yes }
			}
			MAF = {
				country_event = gerdom.502
			}
		}
		if = {

				GEA = { exists = yes }
			}
			GEA = {
				country_event = gerdom.502
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MAG = { exists = yes is_in_faction_with = GER }
			}
			MAG = {
				country_event = gerdom.502
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # War has Gotten So Much Worse

country_event = { # Motors Event
	id = gerdom.720
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.720" }
	title = gerdom.720.t
	desc = gerdom.720.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Elektromotoren
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Excellent
		name = gerdom.720.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER.GER_electrical_cooperation_var
			value = 1
			tooltip = increase_siemens_influence_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER.GER_cartels_dockyard_output
			value = 0.05
			tooltip = Motors_Siemens_Choice_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { # Too much Siemens
					var = GER_electrical_cooperation_var
					value = 3
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.730
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Excellent
		name = gerdom.720.b
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER.GER_electrical_cooperation_var
			value = 1
			tooltip = increase_aeg_influence_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = GER.GER_cartels_consumer_goods
			value = -0.05
			tooltip = Motors_AEG_Choice_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { # Too much AEG
					var = GER_electrical_cooperation_var
					value = -3
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = gerdom.731
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_idea = GER_KWI_Haber_Practicality_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_KWI_Haber_Practicality_idea
				add_idea = GER_KWI_Haber_Practicality_Leipzig_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_KWI_Haber_Innovative_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_KWI_Haber_Innovative_idea
				add_idea = GER_KWI_Haber_Innovative_Leipzig_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_KWI_Planck_Practicality_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_KWI_Planck_Practicality_idea
				add_idea = GER_KWI_Planck_Practicality_Leipzig_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_KWI_Planck_Innovative_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_KWI_Planck_Innovative_idea
				add_idea = GER_KWI_Planck_Innovative_Leipzig_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_KWI_Bieberbach_Practicality_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_KWI_Bieberbach_Practicality_idea
				add_idea = GER_KWI_Bieberbach_Practicality_Leipzig_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_KWI_Bieberbach_Innovative_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_KWI_Bieberbach_Innovative_idea
				add_idea = GER_KWI_Bieberbach_Innovative_Leipzig_idea
			}
		}

# Cosmetic Change for GEX
country_event = {
	id = gerfla.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerfla.11" }
	title = gerfla.11.t
	desc = gerfla.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GEX
		NOT = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = GER
		}
		OR = {
			64 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				} #Brandenburg - Berlin
			55 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				} #Hessen - Frankfurt
			59 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				} #Hannover - Hamburg
			51 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				} #Ostrheinland - Essen
			52 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				} #Oberbayern - Munich
		}
		always = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = gerfla.11.a
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GEX_becomes_GER

		if = {
			limit = {
				64 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_capital = { state = 64 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				55 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_capital = { state = 55 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				59 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_capital = { state = 59 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				51 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_capital = { state = 51 }
		}
		else = {
			set_capital = { state = 52 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.african_tags_array = GEX } }
			remove_from_array = { global.african_tags_array = GEX }
			add_to_array = { global.european_tags_array = GEX }
		}
	}
}

		add_political_power = -15
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = gerfla.45
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gerfla.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerfla.200" }
	title = gerfla.200.t
	desc = gerfla.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Zeppelin

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = gerfla.200.a
		780 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = air_base
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		64 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = air_base
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		set_technology = {
			airships1 = 1
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = heavy_airship_equipment_0 amount = 6 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					NOT = { tag = GER }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = gerfla.202
					days = 120
				}
			}
			INT = { country_event = { id = gerfla.203 days = 150 } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = gerfla.203 days = 150 } }
			RUS = { country_event = { id = gerfla.203 days = 150 } }
			USA = { country_event = { id = gerfla.203 days = 150 } }
		}
	}
}
